<drf|laptop> 03How do you rip into the MOGG container?
<drf|laptop> 03Assuming you're using the same method as everybody else, you'd be recording it uncompressed (as far as I know, all digital audio editors use uncompressed until your final export). All you have to do is save those as WAV - I pair them as stereo rather than one huge multi-track file (this is actually more ideal anyway, since the MOGGs you have to make stereo pairs each time you open it)
<drf|laptop> 03I use FLAC (command-line program) to compress the WAVs. But I'm fine with WAV too - it just takes longer to upload and download... FLAC is like a ZIP file, it can be up to 40-50% smaller.
<drf|laptop> 03Also, FLAC *is* mathematically lossless. It's like taking a WAV file and compressing it in a .zip archive. There technically IS such a thing as lossy FLAC but you only get that using third-party compressors.
